var oldAnim = $.fn.animate;
$.fn.animate = function(prop){
    if('background-position' in prop){
        prop.backgroundPosition = prop['background-position'];
        delete prop['background-position'];
    }
    if('backgroundPosition' in prop){
        prop.backgroundPosition = '('+ prop.backgroundPosition + ')';
    }
    return oldAnim.apply(this, arguments);
};

function toArray(strg){
    strg = strg.replace(/left|top/g,'0px');
    strg = strg.replace(/right|bottom/g,'100%');
    strg = strg.replace(/([0-9\.]+)(\s|\)|$)/g,"$1px$2");
    var res = strg.match(/(-?[0-9\.]+)(px|\%|em|pt)\s(-?[0-9\.]+)(px|\%|em|pt)/);
    if (res && res[1]){
        return [parseFloat(res[1],10),res[2],parseFloat(res[3],10),res[4]];
    }
    return null;

}

			<script>
				var winW = $(window).width();
				if(winW<1680){
					$('.dis_pic').hide();
					$('.change_p').eq(0).addClass('cl');
					$('.change_p').addClass('cur');
					picShow()
				}
				
				function picShow(){
					$('.change_p').hover(function(){
						var picIndex = $(this).index('.change_p');
						$('.change_pic').hide();
						$('.change_pic').eq(picIndex).show();
						$('.change_p').removeClass('cl');
						$('.change_p').eq(picIndex).addClass('cl')
					})
				}

			$(function(){
				window.onload = window.onresize = window.onscroll = function ()
				{
					var oBox = document.getElementById("menu");
					var iScrollTop = document.documentElement.scrollTop || document.body.scrollTop;
					setTimeout(function ()
					{
					clearInterval(oBox.timer);
					var iTop = parseInt((document.documentElement.clientHeight - oBox.offsetHeight)/5) + iScrollTop + 50;
					oBox.timer = setInterval(function ()
					{
					var iSpeed = (iTop - oBox.offsetTop) / 8;
					iSpeed = iSpeed > 0 ? Math.ceil(iSpeed) : Math.floor(iSpeed);
					oBox.offsetTop == iTop ? clearInterval(oBox.timer) : (oBox.style.top = oBox.offsetTop + iSpeed  + "px");
					}, 30)
					}, 100)
										
						var oBox1 = document.getElementById("menu1");
					var iScrollTop1 = document.documentElement.scrollTop || document.body.scrollTop;
					setTimeout(function ()
					{
					clearInterval(oBox1.timer);
					var iTop1 = parseInt((document.documentElement.clientHeight - oBox1.offsetHeight)/5) + iScrollTop1 + 50;
					oBox1.timer = setInterval(function ()
					{
					var iSpeed1 = (iTop1 - oBox1.offsetTop) / 8;
					iSpeed1 = iSpeed1 > 0 ? Math.ceil(iSpeed1) : Math.floor(iSpeed1);
					oBox1.offsetTop == iTop1 ? clearInterval(oBox1.timer) : (oBox1.style.top = oBox1.offsetTop + iSpeed1  + "px");
					}, 30)
					}, 100)
				};
				
				
				$('.change_top').click(function(){
					$('body,html').animate({scrollTop:0},300)
				});
				

				
				
			})
		</script>

					} else {

					for(var a = 0, len1 = dataInfo1.length; a < len1; a++) {

							url1 = dataInfo1[a].url;

								'href': url1,

							});

						loadData(url);
						$(this).parents('.box_title').find('.tab_province a').html($(e.target).html());

					}
				})

				function loadData(url, fn) {
					$.ajax({
						type: "get",
						url: url,
						dataType: "xml",
						error: function(xml) {
							//alert("åŠ è½½XML æ–‡ä»¶å‡ºé”™!");
						},
						success: function(xml) {
							var html = '';
							$(xml).find("item").each(function(i) {
								var title = $(this).find("title").text();
								var href = $(this).find("id").text();
								var time = $(this).find("time").text();
								var pic = $(this).find("pic").text();
								html += '<li><a href=' + href + ' target="_blank">' + title + '</a></li>';
							})
							newsC.html(html);
							fn && fn();
						}
					})
				}

			});
		</script>

					var lxxindex = $(this).index();
					/*liçš„boxçš„index*/
					var lxxindex1 = $(this).parents('.lxx-box').index();

					if(lxxindex1 > 8) {
						lxxindex1 = 8;
					} else if(lxxindex1 > 4) {
						lxxindex1 = lxxindex1 - 1;
					}
					/*ç‚¹å‡»liçš„boxçš„å®šä½*/
					var a = $('.lxx-box').eq(lxxindex).attr('id');
					/*åŸboxçš„å®šä½*/
					var b = $('.lxx-box').eq(lxxindex1).attr('id');
					/*æ”¹å˜boxçš„ä½ç½®*/
					$('.lxx-box').eq(lxxindex).attr('id', b)
					$('.lxx-box').eq(lxxindex1).attr('id', a)

					var ids = []
					$('.lxx-box').each(function(i, n) {
						ids.push($(this).attr('id'));
					});

					$.cookie('ids', ids);
				});

			function addScript(url) {
				for(var index = 0; index < url.length; index++) {
					var element = url[index];
					var scriptObj = document.createElement("script");
					scriptObj.src = element;
					scriptObj.type = "text/javascript";
					document.getElementsByTagName("body")[0].appendChild(scriptObj);
				}
			}
